**Important Considerations for Stacking:**

Remember that bonuses of the same type do not stack [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHfqcMJGlNNowMvVpN17zQvcXHIvQ6CBmQeU0VHNiuodleO_fKTVxqBbZr4Be28uvg3-Tph9pQpkSpvVrqf7I23zymFCMdao7Yo2-Ywkid6I0aQE92trx4gU_GaP9bkgw4OFA==). You can only use the highest bonus of each type (circumstance, item, status) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQHfqcMJGlNNowMvVpN17zQvcXHIvQ6CBmQeU0VHNiuodleO_fKTVxqBbZr4Be28uvg3-Tph9pQpkSpvVrqf7I23zymFCMdao7Yo2-Ywkid6I0aQE92trx4gU_GaP9bkgw4OFA==) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/grounding-api-redirect/AUZIYQF_67tsvJhpV_iyUEuF74j7jHejJ5eaxYGAm-LC6SDVAP_Lb4RzG9YtsHV1WkTDRGGTuCj4uSM5zYh5bP_KvVLUmMDYpmmtab4WVJ6vMLStWs_IvLv48eyMa3YN1hTVU4foqAq6VISpuH9ZCiBI0ci4A967sZQvF-Q=). Therefore, to maximize your Will save, you need to find bonuses of *different* types.

--- Research Result 2 ---
In Pathfinder 2e, circumstance bonuses can affect saving throws against spells, including those with mental effects. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [thedmlair](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) [d20pfsrd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) Here's a breakdown of how they work:

**1. Saving Throws and Bonuses**

*   **Types of Saving Throws:** Pathfinder 2e features Fortitude, Reflex, and Will saves. [d20pfsrd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) Will saves are specifically used to resist attacks on the mind and spirit. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)
*   **Bonuses:** When making a saving throw, you add a proficiency bonus, and other bonuses, to your d20 roll. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-7)
*   **Circumstance Bonuses:** These bonuses depend on the situation. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8) For example, being behind cover grants a +2 circumstance bonus to AC. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9) [d20pfsrd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-6)
*   **Stacking:** You can add different types of bonuses (circumstance, item, status) to the same roll. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8) However, multiple bonuses of the same type don't stack; you only use the highest one. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-8) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-9)

**2. Mental Traits and Effects** [thedmlair](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-10) [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)

*   Some spells and effects have the "mental" trait, indicating they affect the mind. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4)
*   A creature might have a circumstance penalty to saving throws against mental effects. [d20pfsrd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-3) [thedmlair](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-4) [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-12) For example, the *City of Sin* spell can impose a -2 or -4 circumstance penalty to saves against mental effects. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-12)
*   *Strength of Mind* spell grants a +1 status bonus to saving throws against mental effects. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2) This bonus increases to +2 if the source of the effect has the fear trait.

**3. Examples of Circumstance Bonuses in Play**

*   The *Courageous Anthem* cantrip provides a +1 status bonus to saves against fear effects. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11)
*   The *Mind of Menace* spell can grant a +2 status bonus to your saving throw against a triggering mental effect. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0)

**4. Conditions and Mental Effects** [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-13)

*   Conditions themselves generally don't have traits. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-13)
*   However, abilities that inflict conditions often have traits like "fear" and "mental," which can interact with immunities. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-13) For example, a *Fear* spell has the Fear, Emotion, and Mental traits. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-13) [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11)

**5. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11) Specific Spells and Abilities**

*   **Befuddler:** This creature has an ability called "Mental Enchanter" that grants a +1 circumstance bonus to the spell's rank when it casts a mental spell that targets a single creature. [thedmlair](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1)
*   **Psychic Class:** The Psychic class has abilities that can grant bonuses to saving throws against mental effects. [github](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-11) [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5) [thedmlair](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) For example, the *Restore the Mind* ability can grant an ally a +1 status bonus to saving throws against mental effects. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-5)

In summary, circumstance bonuses can indeed improve your saving throws against mental effects in Pathfinder 2e. These bonuses, along with status and item bonuses, are added to your saving throw roll. Certain spells and abilities can provide specific bonuses against mental effects or fear effects, further enhancing your defenses. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-2)


--- Research Result 3 ---
In Pathfinder 2nd Edition, saving throws are a fundamental mechanic for resisting harmful effects. Here's a breakdown of how they work and how circumstance bonuses can apply, especially against mental effects:

**1. [roll20](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) Saving Throw Basics**

*   **Types:** There are three main types of saving throws: [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)
    *   **Fortitude:** Resists effects that debilitate the body, using your Constitution modifier. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)
    *   **Reflex:** Measures your ability to react quickly and avoid effects, using your Dexterity modifier. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)
    *   **Will:** Resists attacks on your mind and spirit, using your Wisdom modifier. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)
*   **The Roll:** To make a saving throw, you roll a d20 and add relevant modifiers. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) The goal is to meet or exceed the Difficulty Class (DC) of the effect. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [pathfinder2e](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6)
*   **Proficiency:** You always add a proficiency bonus to each saving throw, which depends on your training level (Trained, Expert, Master, Legendary).
*   **Formula:** The general formula for a saving throw is: d20 roll + ability modifier + proficiency bonus + other bonuses + penalties.
*   **Degrees of Success:** The outcome of a saving throw can be a critical success, success, failure, or critical failure, each with different effects. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)

**2. [paizo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) Bonuses to Saving Throws**

*   **Types of Bonuses:** Several types of bonuses can apply to saving throws:
    *   **Circumstance Bonuses:** These depend on the situation. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [paizo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
    *   **Status Bonuses:** These reflect your current state (e.g., from a spell or condition).
    *   **Item Bonuses:** These come from equipment like resilient armor or magic items. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4)
*   **Stacking:** You add different types of bonuses together. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [rpg](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) However, if you have multiple bonuses of the same type, only the highest one applies. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4)

**3. Will Saves and Mental Effects** [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [paizo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2)

*   **Will Saves:** Will saves are specifically used to resist mental effects, which target your mind and spirit. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)
*   **Classes and Will Saves:** Classes determine your proficiency in each saving throw, and some classes might grant higher proficiency in Will saves. [quora](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) For example, the Psychic class is trained in Fortitude and Reflex saves but is an expert in Will saves. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8)
*   **Circumstance Bonuses to Will Saves:** Certain abilities, spells, or items can grant circumstance bonuses to Will saves against mental effects.

**4. [paizo](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) Examples of Circumstance Bonuses Against Mental Effects**

*   **Regalia - Adept (Class Feature):** The Regalia-Adept grants a +1 status bonus to all saving throws against mental effects. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-11)
*   **Mind of Menace (Spell):** Grants the "Fight with Fear" reaction, which imposes a Will save on a creature using a mental effect against you. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12) On a failure, the creature is frightened, and you gain a +2 status bonus to your saving throw against the triggering mental effect. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12)
*   **Serene Mutagen (Item):** Provides an item bonus to Will saves, which improves when attempting Will saves against mental effects. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [rpg](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
*   **Psychic Class:** An ally can gain a +1 status bonus to saving throws against mental effects until your psyche ends. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8)
*   **Changeling Called (Feat):** Will saves vs mental effects get +1 and upgrade success. [rpg](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)

**5. Other Considerations**

*   **Conditions:** Certain conditions, like being prone or frightened, can impose penalties on saving throws.
*   **Spells and Abilities:** Many spells and abilities can affect saving throws, either by imposing penalties on the target or granting bonuses to the character making the save.
*   **Mindless Creatures:** Mindless creatures and those with rudimentary intelligence are often immune to mental damage and effects. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4)


--- Research Result 4 ---
It appears you're asking about ways to gain a stacking circumstance bonus to Will saves against mental effects in Pathfinder 2e. Here's a breakdown of what the search results indicate:

**1. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) Stacking Bonuses in Pathfinder 2e**

*   Bonuses of the same type generally do not stack. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) You only use the highest bonus of that type. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1) (e.g., If you have two item bonuses, you only apply the higher one). [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-2) [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)
*   However, bonuses of *different* types (circumstance, item, status, proficiency) *do* stack.

**2. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) Circumstance Bonuses**

*   Circumstance bonuses are situational. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Using the "Aid" action can grant an ally a +1 circumstance bonus to a skill check or attack roll. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)
*   Taking cover can grant a circumstance bonus to AC. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-3)

**3. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) Specific Class Features, Feats, and Spells**

*   **Bloomguard (Feat):** Grants a +2 circumstance bonus to Will saves and Will DCs against mental effects and effects created by fey. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4) Also, once per day, you can roll twice and take the better result on a save against a mental effect or an effect created by a fey. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-4)
*   **Inspiring Resilience (Feat):** Grants allies within 30 feet a +1 circumstance bonus to their Will save against an effect with the emotion, fear, or mental trait. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-5) This bonus increases to +2 if the effect originates from an undead.
*   **Mind of Menace (Spell):**  A 3rd-level spell that, when triggered by a creature using a mental effect against you, can impose the frightened condition on the triggering creature and grant you a +2 status bonus to your saving throw against that effect. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-6)
*   **Commander's Banner (Commander Class Feature):** Provides a +1 status bonus to Will saving throws and DCs against fear effects to allies within the banner's aura. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7) At level 20, the Glorious Banner feat increases this bonus against fear to +2 and adds a +1 status bonus to AC, Fortitude saves, and Reflex saves. Enemies in the aura take a -2 status penalty to Will saves. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)
*   **Serene Mutagen (Item):** Provides an item bonus to Will saves, which is higher against mental effects. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-8) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-9) Some versions also upgrade the result of a successful Will save against a mental effect to a critical success.

**4. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0) Other potentially relevant abilities & items**

*   **Throneglass Armor:** Standard-grade armor grants a +2 circumstance bonus to saving throws against mental effects. [pf2](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-10) [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-0)
*   **Greater Resolve (Class Feature):** At level 17, this class feature increases your Will save proficiency to legendary and upgrades successful Will saves to critical successes. [demiplane](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-11)
*   **Mental Static (Psychic Feat):** If you critically succeed on a Will save against a mental effect, you can use a reaction to inflict mental damage on the originator. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12)
*   **Mental Balm (Psychic Amp):** Provides +2 to emotion saves for 1 minute, and can counteract fear or stupefy. [reddit](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-12) [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-13)
*   **Courageous Anthem (Cantrip):** Grants a +1 status bonus to saves against fear effects. [youtube](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-7)

**Important Considerations:**

*   **Type Matters:** Remember that only bonuses of *different* types will stack. You can't stack multiple circumstance bonuses. [aonprd](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/3-1)
*   **Specific vs. General:** Some bonuses might apply only to specific types of mental effects (e.g., fear).

It is important to consult the specific rules for each ability, feat, or spell in the Pathfinder 2e rulebooks or on Archives of Nethys to understand the exact mechanics and limitations.
